#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x7EE0 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x7EE1 [0x45] LOAD_SCHEDULED_TASK: Load scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=[200*, 0*]
  2: 0x7EF2 [0x55] WAIT_LOAD_SCHEDULER: Wait for scheduler "fdo1" with entities [LocalPlayer, LocalPlayer], work=200*
  3: 0x7F01 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  4: 0x7F03 [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=19*)
```
